# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Kubernetes Storage Subsystem CSI Driver Integration

## Your Task

Find all Go source files in kubernetes/kubernetes that implement the CSI driver integration: the CSI node plugin client, the CSI volume attach/detach controller, the CSI volume provisioner, and the PersistentVolume controller that bridges CSI operations to the core storage API.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the org domain.

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kubernetes--v1.32.0, sg-evals/client-go--v0.32.0, sg-evals/api--v0.32.0, sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd` (etcd-io/etcd)

## Summary of Findings

The file identifies **18 key Go source files** implementing the complete CSI driver integration:

### Core CSI Components (pkg/volume/csi/):
- **csi_plugin.go** - Main CSI plugin with RegistrationHandler
- **csi_client.go** - gRPC client interface to CSI drivers with NodePublishVolume, NodeUnpublishVolume, NodeStageVolume, NodeUnstageVolume operations
- **csi_drivers_store.go** - Registry of installed CSI drivers
- **csi_attacher.go** - Attach/Detach implementation (volume.Attacher, volume.Detacher)
- **csi_mounter.go** - Mount/Unmount operations (Setup, TearDownAt)
- **csi_block.go** - Block device volume handling
- **csi_metrics.go** - Metrics collection
- **expander.go** - Volume expansion operations
- **csi_util.go** - Utility functions

### Node Information Management:
- **nodeinfomanager/nodeinfomanager.go** - CSI driver registration on nodes, managing CSINode objects and topology labels

### Attach/Detach Controller:
- **attach_detach_controller.go** - Main controller managing cluster-wide volume attachment/detachment
- **reconciler/reconciler.go** - Reconciliation logic executing attach/detach operations

### PersistentVolume Controller (CSI Provisioning Bridge):
- **pv_controller.go** - Dynamic provisioning of CSI volumes with provisionClaimOperationExternal()
- **pv_controller_base.go** - CSI translator setup for in-tree to CSI migration

### Storage API:
- **staging/src/k8s.io/api/storage/v1/types.go** - CSIDriver, CSINode, and VolumeAttachment API types

csiPlugin (csi_plugin.go) is the main CSI plugin implementing the Kubernetes volume plugin interface. It includes a RegistrationHandler that validates and registers new CSI drivers when they become available. The csi_plugin.go file is responsible for plugin initialization and lifecycle management. The csiDriverClient (csi_client.go) encapsulates the gRPC communication with CSI drivers, implementing the csiClient interface with methods like NodePublishVolume, NodeUnpublishVolume, NodeStageVolume, and NodeUnstageVolume for node-side operations. The DriversStore (csi_drivers_store.go) maintains a registry of all CSI drivers installed on the node.\\n\\n**Node Plugin Operations (pkg/volume/csi/)**:\\nThe csiAttacher (csi_attacher.go) implements the Attach/Detach operations, calling the CSI driver's node operations. The expander.go implements volume expansion operations, and csi_metrics.go provides metrics collection for CSI volumes.\\n\\n**Node Information Management (pkg/volume/csi/nodeinfomanager/)**:\\nThe nodeInfoManager (nodeinfomanager.go) registers CSI drivers on nodes by updating both Node and CSINode objects. It implements the AttachDetachController interface and coordinates with CSI drivers through the volume plugin interface. The reconciler (reconciler/reconciler.go) executes the attach/detach operations by calling the Attach() and Detach() methods on the csiAttacher.\\n\\n**PersistentVolume Controller (pkg/controller/volume/persistentvolume/)**:\\nThe PersistentVolumeController (pv_controller.go) bridges CSI operations to the core storage API, handling dynamic provisioning of CSI-backed volumes. The pv_controller_base.go sets up the CSI translator for migrating in-tree volumes to CSI. The provisionClaimOperationExternal() function calls external provisioners for CSI volumes.\\n\\n**Storage API Types (staging/src/k8s.io/api/storage/v1/)**:\\nThe types.go file defines CSIDriver, CSINode, and VolumeAttachment objects that coordinate CSI operations. CSI driver integration comprises multiple interconnected components that manage container storage interface volumes across the cluster:\\n\\n**CSI Plugin and Core Components (pkg/volume/csi/)**:\\nThe csiPlugin (csi_plugin.go) is the main CSI plugin implementing the Kubernetes volume plugin interface. It includes a RegistrationHandler that validates and registers new CSI drivers when they become available. The csi_plugin.go file is responsible for plugin initialization and lifecycle management. The csiDriverClient (csi_client.go) encapsulates the gRPC communication with CSI drivers, implementing the csiClient interface with methods like NodePublishVolume, NodeUnpublishVolume, NodeStageVolume, and NodeUnstageVolume for node-side operations. The DriversStore (csi_drivers_store.go) maintains a registry of all CSI drivers installed on the node.\\n\\n**Node Plugin Operations (pkg/volume/csi/)**:\\nThe csiAttacher (csi_attacher.go) implements the Attach/Detach operations, calling the CSI driver's node operations. The csiMountMgr (csi_mounter.go) handles mounting and unmounting of volumes, implementing Setup() and TearDownAt() methods. The csiBlockMapper (csi_block.go) manages block device volumes. The expander.go implements volume expansion operations, and csi_metrics.go provides metrics collection for CSI volumes.\\n\\n**Node Information Management (pkg/volume/csi/nodeinfomanager/)**:\\nThe nodeInfoManager (nodeinfomanager.go) registers CSI drivers on nodes by updating both Node and CSINode objects. The Interface defines methods like InstallCSIDriver() and UninstallCSIDriver() that manage the CSINode object with driver information, topology labels, and volume attachment limits.\\n\\n**Attach/Detach Controller (pkg/controller/volume/attachdetach/)**:\\nThe attachDetachController (attach_detach_controller.go) is the main controller managing volume attachment and detachment across the cluster. It implements the AttachDetachController interface and coordinates with CSI drivers through the volume plugin interface. The reconciler (reconciler/reconciler.go) executes the attach/detach operations by calling the Attach() and Detach() methods on the csiAttacher.\\n\\n**PersistentVolume Controller (pkg/controller/volume/persistentvolume/)**:\\nThe PersistentVolumeController (pv_controller.go) bridges CSI operations to the core storage API, handling dynamic provisioning of CSI-backed volumes. The pv_controller_base.go sets up the CSI translator for migrating in-tree volumes to CSI. The provisionClaimOperationExternal() function calls external provisioners for CSI volumes.\\n\\n**Storage API Types (staging/src/k8s.io/api/storage/v1/)**:\\nThe types.go file defines CSIDriver, CSINode, and VolumeAttachment objects that coordinate CSI operations. VolumeAttachment objects capture the intent to attach/detach volumes and track the attachment status managed by external CSI attachers.\\n\\n**Integration Flow**:\\n1. CSI drivers register through the RegistrationHandler.RegisterPlugin() in csi_plugin.go\\n2. Node information is updated via nodeinfomanager.InstallCSIDriver()\\n3. The attachDetachController.NewAttachDetachController() creates the main controller\\n4. Volume attachments are managed through the reconciler.reconcileVolumes()\\n5. PersistentVolumeController.provisionClaimOperationExternal() handles CSI volume provisioning\\n6. csiAttacher.Attach() and Detach() interface with the CSI drivers through csiDriverClient\\n7. Mount/unmount operations proceed through csiMountMgr in csi_mounter.go\"\n}"
